#Consolidated the 100+ SWMH files here to clean this folder up

#For easy copy paste for now
#Here are the formatting instructions:
#
#This is the first input. I will give you something that looks like follows:
#
#1000035571 = {
#name="Siconidi"
#prefix = "dynnp_di"
# culture = italian
#}
#
#You would then do the following edit:
#
#1000035571 = {
#name="dynn_Siconidi"
#prefix = "dynnp_di"
# culture = italian
#}
#
#Always add the dynn_ prefix to this first outputs name. Always remove special characters and replace them with a corresponding latin character. For example ò is replaced with o. NEVER leave special characters in this part. If there are spaces for the name replace them with underscores.
#
#I then want you to do ANOTHER output which is the localization output. 
# 
#For example:
#
#dynn_Siconidi:0 "Siconidi" 
#
#Where the text in the quotes is the localized text. Most importantly that localized text is the ONLY PLACE special characters should be maintained. In cases where there is a space in the name I want you to use underscores but DO NOT put those underscores in the localized text output.
#
#
#
#
#This is an example of how to handle special characters: 
#
#1000035642 = {
#name="Angiò"
#prefix = "dynnp_d_"
# culture = neapolitan
#}
#
#would become 
#
#1000035642 = {
#name="dynn_Angio"
#prefix = "dynnp_d_"
# culture = neapolitan
#}
#
#and it's localized output would be 
#
#dynn_Angio:0 "Angiò"
#
#
#Always do these 2 outputs with the rules I have given and always do the outputs with all of the first part together and all of the second part together.

1062290 = {
	# Modern: Ság; etymologically unclear, but likely to be a Khavar clan name
	name = "Sag" # Was Nyék, but Nýek dynasty already exists
	culture = mogyer # Was hungarian
}
1062291 = {
	# Modern: Varsány
	name = "Varsaný" # Was Tarján, but Tarian dynasty already exists
	culture = mogyer # Was hungarian
}
1062292 = {
	# Modern: Tolmács; from "Talmács", a Pecheneg clan name
	name = "Talmac" # Was Jenó, but Ieney dynasty already exists
	culture = mogyer # Was hungarian
}
1062293 = {
	# Modern: Eszlár; actually a variant of "Úz", i.e. Oghuz
	name = "Uzlar" # Was Kér, but Keri dynasty already exists
	culture = mogyer # Was hungarian
}
1062294 = {
	# Modern: Ladány
	name = "Ladaný" # Was Megyer, but Meger dynasty already exists
